  //<![CDATA[
    function loadScript(url, callback) {
      var script = document.createElement("script");
      script.type = "text/javascript";
    
      if (script.readyState) {  //Internet Explorer
          script.onreadystatechange = function() {
            if (script.readyState == "loaded" ||
                    script.readyState == "complete") {
              script.onreadystatechange = null;
              callback();
            }
          };
      } else {  //Other browsers
        script.onload = function() {
          callback();
        };
      }
    
      script.src = url;
      document.getElementsByTagName("head")[0].appendChild(script);
    }
    
    function initAppleId() {
      AppleID.auth.init({
        clientId : 'com.goodreads.app', 
        scope : 'name email',
        redirectURI: 'https://www.goodreads.com/apple_users/sign_in_with_apple_web',
        state: 'apple_oauth_state_a558a83b-82c6-4589-bd6d-a69e7e7f37bd'
      });
    }

        }
      });
      $('rating_details_tip').observe('prototip:hidden', function () {
        $$('span.elementTwo').each(function (e) {
          if (e.getStyle('display') !== 'none') {
            var lessLink = e.next();
            swapContent(lessLink);
          }
        });
      });

It really brings the world of Catching Fire to life and it has a special place on top of my THG shelf!</span>

        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer771710634" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer16705907813671641725">This review appears on <a href='http://www.happyindulgencebooks.com/2013/12/15/aus-giveaway-review-the-hunger-games-catching-fire-official-illustrated-movie-companion/' rel='nofollow noopener'>Happy Indulgence.</a> Check it out for more reviews!<br/><br/>The Catching Fire Official Illustrated Movie Companion is the great way to relive this highly anticipated movie and get behind the scenes insight into how it was put together. Featuring high quality illustrations and movie stills of Catching Fire during its filming, the companion is beautiful to look at and captures the movie perfectly. While I would have liked more insight from the stars – there are some quotes here and ther</span>
  <span id="freeText16705907813671641725" style="display:none">This review appears on <a href="http://www.happyindulgencebooks.com/2013/12/15/aus-giveaway-review-the-hunger-games-catching-fire-official-illustrated-movie-companion/" rel="nofollow noopener">Happy Indulgence.</a> Check it out for more reviews!<br /><br />The Catching Fire Official Illustrated Movie Companion is the great way to relive this highly anticipated movie and get behind the scenes insight into how it was put together. Featuring high quality illustrations and movie stills of Catching Fire during its filming, the companion is beautiful to look at and captures the movie perfectly. While I would have liked more insight from the stars – there are some quotes here and there about the production of the movie – the companion goes into depth about how the locations in Panem and the Cornucopia Arena were put together, and the costume and makeup for the actors. It helps you appreciate the thought process and the different elements that make up a movie, which perfectly contributed to its feeling and characterisation.<br /><br />I liked how the fashion designer described her decisions behind putting together Katniss and Effie’s costume choices – Katniss wearing simple garments while in District 12 while she’s slightly more dressed up on the Victory Tour, and Effie’s playfulness, exaggerated character, but also slave to the Capitol comes through her fashion. Interestingly enough, for the first time I noticed the Avoxes, the slaves to the Capitol which apparently appeared in the movie. The casting of Johanna Mason and Plutarch was also interesting to know, as was actually using a real life estate for President’s Snow Mansion.<br /><br />Perfect for fans of the series, The Catching Fire Movie Companion will both delight and offer insights to the best movie released in 2014.<br /><br /><a href="http://ibrary.tumblr.com/post/68110601282/catching-fire-movie-review-jeann-wong" rel="nofollow noopener">Click here</a> for my movie review of Catching Fire! </span>
  <a data-text-id="16705907813671641725" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

<div id="review_1113290343" class="review" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/1113290343" />
    <a title="Sharon Powers" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/30801573-sharon-powers"><img alt="Sharon Powers" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1431988633p2/30801573.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/1113290343?book_show_action=true">Nov 23, 2014</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Sharon Powers" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Sharon Powers" href="/user/show/30801573-sharon-powers">Sharon Powers</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="really liked it"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">really liked it</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>



        

    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer1113290343" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer6515130660249801981">Book Review by Sharon Powers.<br/><br/>If you would like to see the entire review with graphics, References/sources, the go to <a target='_blank' rel='noopener nofollow' href='http://sharonsloveofbooks.blogspot.com/'>http://sharonsloveofbooks.blogspot.com/</a><br/>________________________________________________<br/><br/>THE HUNGER GAMES: CATCHING FIRE <br/>THE OFFICIAL ILLUSTRATED MOVIE COMPANION:<br/><br/> The companion book is organized into six parts:<br/>(1) The Hunger Games Catches Fire;<br/>(2) Moving Forward;<br/>(3) Expanding the World of Panem;<br/>(4) Designing the Arena;<br/>(5) Creating Costumes, Designing Faces; and,<br/>(6) Looking Ahead.<br/><br/> Pa</span>
  <span id="freeText6515130660249801981" style="display:none">Book Review by Sharon Powers.<br /><br />If you would like to see the entire review with graphics, References/sources, the go to <a target="_blank" rel="noopener nofollow" href="http://sharonsloveofbooks.blogspot.com/">http://sharonsloveofbooks.blogspot.com/</a><br />________________________________________________<br /><br />THE HUNGER GAMES: CATCHING FIRE <br />THE OFFICIAL ILLUSTRATED MOVIE COMPANION:<br /><br /> The companion book is organized into six parts:<br />(1) The Hunger Games Catches Fire;<br />(2) Moving Forward;<br />(3) Expanding the World of Panem;<br />(4) Designing the Arena;<br />(5) Creating Costumes, Designing Faces; and,<br />(6) Looking Ahead.<br /><br /> Part one reaches back to book 1, The Hunger Games, to speak about the phenomenon of the book and movie. Then the chapter moves on to the continued story of Catching Fire. Here the author explains that Katniss is now a veteran, but still wants to protect those she loves and is "awake," now; even so, Katniss is still not ready to lead.<br /><br /> Part two showcases how the director was so important to the filming of the story, and then went on to tell how the casting was accomplished by considering actors from all over the world. Also, the importance of some of the character's roles was stressed, for example, Plutarch Heavensbee, the mentor, Haymitch, and Finnick and Mags.<br /><br /> Part three, tells the story of how the filmmakers put the world of Panem together, how it was imagined, the logistics of filming, and how continuity was incorporated without losing the individuality of the various districts. Also in this chapter, the Presidential Feast is highlighted along with the setting, The Swan House in Atlanta.<br /><br /> Part four, Designing the Arena, of course, reveals how the company first searched out an appropriate location, but how they worked with the limitations set upon them. The cornucopia and its creation is explained, along with a number of photographs, and then how it was set into the arena as the center of the dial of a clock. Covering the aspect that a true tropical forest setting was needed, the filming in Hawaii and the challenges of the arena filming were, likewise, covered. We also get to see "Life on the Set," and how the actors got to intermingle.<br /><br /> Part five covered, in detail, the creation of the costumes and how certain looks were created for Katniss, Gale Hawthorne, for Katniss's wedding dress, Peeta Mellark's changing look, Cinna, Finnick, Effie Trinket, the Avoxes, Haymitch Abernathy, President Snow, Plutarch Heavensbee, and the uniforms for the games. The challenges of creating a look for each actor were discussed, as well as the problems with functionality of the uniforms.<br /><br /> In Part six, the last chapter, discusses how in the first book we were introduced to Katniss and got to know her and who she is. Then, in Catching Fire, the metaphor that Katniss is a "burning ember" that starts the fire of revolution. And lastly, how in Mockingjay, how the Capitol will feel the "wrath" of the districts. (p.154.)<br /><br />CONCLUSION OF MOVIE GUIDE:<br /> Like the companion guide to The Hunger Games that I reviewed in my last post, I thoroughly enjoyed this book. Here, we get to see a bit more of what happens behind the scenes, what goes on on the set, and how the actors relate to each other. In addition I liked learning more about the motivations of some of the characters and how book two is really fleshing out the story of Katniss. I really liked that the focus was on Katniss's growth of her character. I give this guide 4.0 stars out of 5.<br /><br />______________________________________________________<br /></span>
  <a data-text-id="6515130660249801981" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

  <span id="freeText921901851851535918" style="display:none">"“Catching Fire: The Official Illustrated Movie Companion"” by Kate Egan is a book that will appeal to all fans of the popular movie, primarily because of the abundance of information that can be found inside, but also due to the superiorly designed edition in which they are packed.<br /><br />As is the case with majority of the movie guides itÂ’ recommended that you use it once you see the movie, particularly if you havenÂ’t read the book or you will come across many spoilers that will partially spoil the pleasure of movie watching.<br />Especially can be emphasized the depth with which the author approaches Hunger Games worldwide phenomenon giving plenty of information about most important characters which participate in a brutal game that takes place in the not so beautiful vision of the human future.<br /><br />Besides providing plenty of information about movie production, including many photographs that provide full overview on movie making, this guide also adds lot of behind-the-scene material that the Catching Fire movie fans will especially appreciate, together with explanation of some symbols that are more difficult to notice through the movie while you watch it for the first time.<br />The guide is delivered in quality-made glossy paper that raises the visual appearance of the book making it look more expensive and professional.<br /><br />Therefore, if you'’re a fan of the literary trilogy and/or Hunger Games movie(s) I believe that youÂ’ll like this guide that in very nicely designed release provides a lot of information.</span>

        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer775211285" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer8715981189328701628">This glossy magazine style companion is simply gorgeous. It discusses in depth from the release of The Hunger Games being an instant sensation, the characters of Katniss, Peeta and Gale now being household names. The story of a girl who volunteered as tribute, in order to save her sister Primrose in what would have been her eventual death. In a world where those that live in Capitol are indulging in luxurious parties, lavish fashions and an abundance of possessions, those who live within the dis</span>
  <span id="freeText8715981189328701628" style="display:none">This glossy magazine style companion is simply gorgeous. It discusses in depth from the release of The Hunger Games being an instant sensation, the characters of Katniss, Peeta and Gale now being household names. The story of a girl who volunteered as tribute, in order to save her sister Primrose in what would have been her eventual death. In a world where those that live in Capitol are indulging in luxurious parties, lavish fashions and an abundance of possessions, those who live within the districts barely have enough to survive. Katniss is the heroine of the young adult genre and whether your waiting to see Catching Fire in cinemas or want to relive the costumes, the tender moments or the beginning of a rebellion that launched a genre, you need the official movie companion.<br /><br />If you are yet to see the film, the cinematic are simply stunning. The Official Movie Companion offers beautiful high definition images from the Victory Tour, The Quarter Quell and the outlandish fashions of the Capitol. The new arena is incredible, having been shot between Atlanta and Hawaii, to create a realistic tropical environment. How the Cornucopia was inspired by an abandoned Soviet monument, and how the stunning visuals came to be. It's a brilliant insight into the incredible franchise that fans will enjoy over and over again.<br /></span>
  <a data-text-id="8715981189328701628" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>

While there was much I learned about "Catching Fire's" production, I felt that Egan's writing was too simplified, relied too much on actor's interviews, and never went in-depth as much as I would have liked. Of course, the book's target audience is young teenagers, who ar</span>
  <span id="freeText4477831307554563987" style="display:none">This book has many high-quality pictures of the hit film, and includes interesting tidbits about casting, location shoots (arena game was filmed in Hawaii!) and, best of all, an in-depth look at each character's costume design. While there was much I learned about "Catching Fire's" production, I felt that Egan's writing was too simplified, relied too much on actor's interviews, and never went in-depth as much as I would have liked. Of course, the book's target audience is young teenagers, who are not professional cinematic critics, and who have followed the film's production from the beginning anyways, but I would have liked more technical details, particularly concerning director Francis Lawrence's decision-making process. </span>

  function submitShelfLink(unique_id, book_id, shelf_id, shelf_name, submit_form, exclusive) {
    var checkbox_id = 'shelf_name_' + unique_id + '_' + shelf_id;
    var element = document.getElementById(checkbox_id)

    var checked = element.checked
    if (checked && exclusive) {
      // can't uncheck a radio by clicking it!
      return
    }
    if(document.getElementById("savingMessage")){
      Element.show('savingMessage')
    }
    var element_id = 'shelfInDropdownName_' + unique_id + '_' + shelf_id;
    Element.update(element_id, "saving...");
    if (submit_form) {
      Element.hide('shelfDropdown_' + unique_id)
      var form = document.getElementById('addBookForm' + book_id)
      if (form) {
        form.shelf.value = shelf_name
        form.onsubmit()
      }
    }
    else {
      var action = checked ? 'remove' : ''
      element.checked = !element.checked
      new Ajax.Request('/shelf/add_to_shelf', {asynchronous:true, evalScripts:true, onSuccess:function(request){shelfSubmitted(request, book_id, checkbox_id, element_id, unique_id, shelf_name)}, parameters:'book_id=' + book_id + '&name=' + shelf_name + '&a=' + action + '&authenticity_token=' + encodeURIComponent('EEJMQzByL7mV/kMwygJ/dBzaVc8EgC6xx6grC71p2AteheATQrq7qp5+FWcwoB6S/M2/Owf8XpiY9kEDsJqFXw==')})
    }
  }

  function shelfSubmitted(request, book_id, checkbox_id, element_id, unique_id, shelf_name) {
    Element.update('shelfListfalse_' + book_id, request.responseText)
    afterShelfSave(checkbox_id, element_id, unique_id, shelf_name.escapeHTML())
  }

  function refreshGroupBox(group_id, book_id) {
    new Ajax.Updater('addGroupBooks' + book_id + '', '/group/add_book_box', {asynchronous:true, evalScripts:true, onSuccess:function(request){refreshGroupBoxComplete(request, book_id);}, parameters:'id=' + group_id + '&book_id=' + book_id + '&refresh=true' + '&authenticity_token=' + encodeURIComponent('avVYBOAJAhLz6zrMXZAfD31YODMLNj3EHrWiTMvrTzokMvRUksGWAfhrbJunMn7pnU/SxwhKTe1B68hExhgSbg==')})
  }

            if ($('bookCover_20698371').hasClassName('ignored')) {
              e.setStyle({'display': 'none'});
              return;
            }
            e.setStyle({'overflow': 'visible'});
          });
        });
      $('bookCover_20698371').observe('prototip:hidden', function () {
        $$('span.elementTwo').each(function (e) {
          if (e.getStyle('display') !== 'none') {
            var lessLink = e.next();
            swapContent(lessLink);
          }
        });
      });

//]]>
</script>

</li>
</ul>
